                dscp nc1 fc h1 profile in
                dscp nc2 fc nc profile in
                dscp af13 fc l2 profile out
                dscp af23 fc af profile out
                dscp af33 fc l1 profile out
                dscp af41 fc h2 profile in
                dscp af43 fc h2 profile out
                dot1p 1 fc be profile use-de
                dot1p 2 fc l2 profile use-de
                dot1p 3 fc af profile use-de
                dot1p 4 fc l1 profile use-de
                dot1p 5 fc h2 profile use-de
                dot1p 6 fc ef profile use-de
                dot1p 7 fc h1 profile use-de
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc af
                    dscp-in-profile cs3
                    dscp-out-profile af23
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 2
                    dot1p-in-profile 3
                    dot1p-out-profile 3
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 3
                exit
                fc be
                    dscp-out-profile cp1
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 4
                    dot1p-in-profile 1
                    dot1p-out-profile 1
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 1
                exit
                fc ef
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 6
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 6
                    dot1p-in-profile 6
                    dot1p-out-profile 6
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 6
                exit
                fc h1
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 7
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 7
                    dot1p-in-profile 7
                    dot1p-out-profile 7
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 7
                exit
                fc h2
                    dscp-out-profile af43
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 5
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 5
                    dot1p-in-profile 5
                    dot1p-out-profile 5
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 5
                exit
                fc l1
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile af33
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 3
                    dot1p-in-profile 4
                    dot1p-out-profile 4
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 4
                exit
                fc l2
                    dscp-in-profile cs2
                    dscp-out-profile af13
                    dot1p-in-profile 2
                    dot1p-out-profile 2
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 2
                exit
                fc nc
                    de-mark
                    port-redirect-group queue 8
                exit
            exit
        exit
        network 301 name "301" create
            description "SE network QoS policy"
            ingress
                dscp be fc be profile in
                dscp ef fc nc profile in
                dscp cp1 fc be profile out
                dscp cs2 fc l2 profile in
                dscp cs3 fc af profile in
                dscp cs4 fc l1 profile in
                dscp cs5 fc ef profile in
                dscp nc1 fc h1 profile in
                dscp nc2 fc nc profile in
                dscp af13 fc l2 profile in
                dscp af23 fc af profile in
                dscp af33 fc l1 profile in
                dscp af41 fc h2 profile in
                dscp af43 fc h2 profile in
                lsp-exp 0 fc be profile in
                lsp-exp 1 fc l2 profile in
                lsp-exp 2 fc af profile in
                lsp-exp 3 fc l1 profile in
                lsp-exp 4 fc be profile out
                lsp-exp 5 fc h2 profile in
                lsp-exp 6 fc ef profile in
                lsp-exp 7 fc h1 profile in
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc af
                    dscp-in-profile cs3
                    dscp-out-profile cs3
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 2
                exit
                fc be
                    dscp-out-profile cp1
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 4
                exit
                fc ef
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 6
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 6
                exit
                fc h1
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 7
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 7
                exit
                fc h2
                    dscp-out-profile af41
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 5
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 5
                exit
                fc l1
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile cs4
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 3
                exit
                fc l2
                    dscp-in-profile cs2
                    dscp-out-profile cs2
                exit
            exit
        exit
